<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeven.html>uitgeven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to publish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Or alternatively, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgever</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">publisher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also the usage notes at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i>.

***uithangen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a> (6016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utehangen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uuthangen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uythangen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You probably <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a> to <b>hang out</b> the laundry.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to act like, to behave like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">to <b>act like</b> a <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> nazi <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofzo.html>ofzo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duizenden.html>duizenden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Are you now just going to <b>act like</b> a Nazi or what and kill thousands of people?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the sense "to act like", an accompanying noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> always preceded by the definite article, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> when the English equivalent would use an indefinite article. The accompanying noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually singular.
</p>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uithoek.html>uithoek</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to watch (something) until the end</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look out, to watch out, to be vigilant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with "<a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look forward to</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***uitkomen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitkomen.html>uitkomen</a> (3365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utecōmen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitkomen.html>uitkomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to figure out or find a solution for
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadenk.html>nadenk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probleem.html>probleem</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>No matter how long I think about this problem, I <b>can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> figure</b> it <b>out</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come out right, to fit together, to be solvable, to have a result or solution
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:som.html>som</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopt.html>klopt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>This sum isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> right, it doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>come out right</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be fitting, to be (in-)convenient
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>Komt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>?</i>  |  <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a></b> that day <b>convenient</b> for you?  |  No, it <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> actually rather <b>inconvenient</b> for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hatch
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgekomen.html>uitgekomen</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The egg hasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>hatched</b> yet.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come true
<ul><li><b>1994</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:marco.html>Marco</a> Borsato, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dromen.html>Dromen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrog.html>bedrog</a></i>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoveel.html>zoveel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dromen.html>dromen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.
<dl><dd>Once every so often, <a href = vnd.unilang:dreams.html>dreams</a> <b>come true</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Judaism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become Jewish</li></ol>

***uitlaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitlaat.html>uitlaat</a> (13248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">uit-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">útlaat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">outlet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitlaat.html>uitlaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitlaten.html>uitlaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitlaat.html>uitlaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">exhaust</span>, system through which burned gases, steam etc. are vented or otherwise discharged; especially used for a <span class="Latn" lang="en">car</span> exhaust</li>
<li>any <span class="Latn" lang="en">outlet</span>, to relieve pressure, literally and figuratively</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utelaten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl"></span>
</p>
<ol><li>To release, notably:
<ol><li>To liberate, set free</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To unleash (an <a href = vnd.unilang:ogre.html>ogre</a> etc.)</li>
<li>To walk, air (a pet, prisoner...)</li></ol></li>
<li>To lengthen, notably a garment</li>
<li>To abstain from some (usually undesirable) action</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To express oneself</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To publish</li></ol>
